Task instruction sent to agent 
# Implement HyperLogLog Algorithm

**Repository:** bustub (TheAgentCompany GitLab)  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** ccb_tac  
**Task Type:** Algorithm Implementation

## Description

Implement the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the
bustub database system. This requires understanding the existing codebase structure,
following coding conventions, and implementing the algorithm across 4 files.

**Why this benefits from MCP:** 
- bustub is a complex C++ database codebase with specific patterns
- Understanding how other "primer" exercises are implemented provides templates
- Finding similar hash-based data structures shows expected patterns
- Cross-file dependencies between headers and implementations require navigation

## Task

Clone http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace folder and complete 
http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub/-/issues/759 locally. 

Specifically, complete 4 files:
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`

To ensure compatibility of testing across different operating systems, please change 
the line `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` in your local file 
`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h` to:
`hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully  
[x] All 4 implementation files completed  
[x] Unit tests pass (10 tests, graded by pass count)

     1→//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//
     2→//
     3→//                         BusTub
     4→//
     5→// hash_util.h
     6→//
     7→// Identification: src/include/common/util/hash_util.h
     8→//
     9→// Copyright (c) 2015-2025, Carnegie Mellon University Database Group
    10→//
    11→//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//
    12→
    13→#pragma once
    14→
    15→#include <algorithm>
    16→#include <cstdlib>
    17→#include <iostream>
    18→#include <string>
    19→
    20→#include "common/macros.h"
    21→#include "type/value.h"
    22→
    23→namespace bustub {
    24→
    25→using hash_t = std::size_t;
    26→
    27→class HashUtil {
    28→ private:
    29→  static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;
    30→
    31→ public:
    32→  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    33→    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126
    34→    hash_t hash = length;
    35→    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
    36→      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<int8_t>(bytes[i]);
    37→    }
    38→    return hash;
    39→  }
    40→
    41→  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    42→    hash_t both[2] = {};
    43→    both[0] = l;

57-assistanttext-
Now let me analyze the tests to understand exactly what the HyperLogLog implementation needs to do:

1. **Basic HyperLogLog**: 
   - Constructor takes `n_bits` (number of bits for bucket indexing)
   - `AddElem(val)` - adds an element
   - `ComputeCardinality()` - computes and stores cardinality
   - `GetCardinality()` - returns the stored cardinality
   - Needs to support parallelism (thread-safe)

2. **HyperLogLogPresto** (optimized version with dense/overflow buckets):
   - Same interface plus `GetDenseBucket()` and `GetOverflowBucketofIndex(idx)`
   - Uses 4-bit dense buckets with 3-bit overflow buckets

Let me first implement the header file for the basic HyperLogLog, adding necessary member variables:

93-assistanttext-
Looking at EdgeTest2:
- With n_bits=0, we have 2^0 = 1 bucket
- After adding 1, GetCardinality should return 1665180

This means the formula `CONSTANT * m * m / sum` with m=1 and sum = 2^(-register[0]) should give 1665180.

Working backwards: 0.79402 * 1 * 1 / 2^(-x) = 1665180
=> 2^(-x) = 0.79402 / 1665180 = 4.77e-7
=> -x = log2(4.77e-7) = -21.0
=> x = 21

So for value 1, the position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits (which is all 64 bits since n_bits=0) should be 21.

Let me check what hash value 1 produces:

96-assistanttext-

- 0.79402 * 1 * 1 / 2^(-21) = 0.79402 * 2097152 = 1665148.4 ≈ 1665180

The expected cardinality is 1665180, so my position calculation needs to give 21 for the hash of value 1.

The issue in my code is that I'm looking for leading zeros from the wrong direction. Let me trace through my logic:

For n_bits_=0:
- bucket_idx = 0 (always)
- remaining_bits = hash (unchanged, since 0 bits are used for bucket)
- I find position of leftmost 1 from MSB in remaining_bits

209-assistanttext-
The issue is for n=0, mask = 0! That's because 1ULL << 64 is undefined behavior (shifts by ≥64 bits).

Let me fix this:

227-assistanttext-
All 10 tests pass. Let me provide a summary of the implementation:

## Summary

I successfully implemented the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the bustub database system. Here's what was done:

### Files Modified:

1. **`src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`** - Added member variables:
   - `n_bits_` - number of bits for bucket indexing
   - `num_buckets_` - number of buckets (2^n_bits_)
   - `registers_` - vector storing max position for each bucket
   - `mutex_` - for thread safety

2. **`src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`** - Implemented:
   - Constructor initializing buckets
   - `ComputeBinary()` - converts hash to bitset
   - `PositionOfLeftmostOne()` - finds position of leftmost 1 bit from MSB
   - `AddElem()` - thread-safe element addition using bucket from MSB and position from remaining bits
   - `ComputeCardinality()` - HLL formula: α * m² / Σ(2^(-register[i]))

3. **`src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`** - Added member variables:
   - `n_leading_bits_` - number of leading bits for bucket indexing
   - `num_buckets_` - number of buckets

4. **`src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`** - Implemented Presto variant:
   - Uses dense (4-bit) + overflow (3-bit) bucket encoding
   - Bucket index from MSB of hash
   - Position calculated from trailing zeros in remaining bits
   - Dense stores lower 4 bits, overflow stores upper 3 bits of position

### Key Algorithm Details:

**Basic HyperLogLog:**
- Bucket index = top n_bits of hash
- Position = position of leftmost 1 in remaining bits (from MSB)
- Cardinality = 0.79402 * m² / Σ(2^(-M[j]))

**Presto HyperLogLog:**
- Bucket index = top n_leading_bits of hash (from MSB)
- Position = number of trailing zeros in remaining bits
- Total position = (overflow << 4) | dense
- Same cardinality form
... (truncated)

<string>\n\n#include \"common/macros.h\"\n#include \"type/value.h\"\n\nnamespace bustub {\n\nusing hash_t = std::size_t;\n\nclass HashUtil {\n private:\n  static const hash_t PRIME_FACTOR = 10000019;\n\n public:\n  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {\n    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126\n    hash_t hash = length;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {\n      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<int8_t>(bytes[i]);\n    }\n    return hash;\n  }\n\n  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {\n    hash_t both[2] = {};\n    both[0] = l;\n    both[1] = r;\n    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);\n  }\n\n  static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {\n    return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;\n  }\n\n  template <typename T>\n  static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {\n    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));\n  }\n\n static_cast<int64_t>(val->GetAs<int64_t>());\n        return Hash<int64_t>(&raw);\n      }\n      case TypeId::BOOLEAN: {\n        auto raw = val->GetAs<bool>();\n        return Hash<bool>(&raw);\n auto len = val->GetStorageSize();\n        return HashBytes(raw, len);\n      }\n      case TypeId::TIMESTAMP: {\n        auto raw = val->GetAs<uint64_t>();\n        return Hash<uint64_t>(&raw);\n i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      // Position counting from right (LSB=1), so position is i+1\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(i + 1);\n    }\n  }\n  // If all zeros, return BITSET_CAPACITY (max position)\n  return BITSET_CAPACITY;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the first n_bits_ bits (MSB)\n  // The bucket index is taken from the most significant n_bits_ bits\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_bits_; i++) {\n    if (binary.test(BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i)) {\n      bucket_idx |= (static_cast<uint64_t>(1) << (n_bits_ - 1 - i));\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Create a mask to get the remaining bits (excluding the bucket index bits)\n  // We need to find the position of the leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining_bits;\n  for (int i = 0; i < BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_; i++) {\n    remaining_bits[i] = binary[i];\n  }\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t position = 0;\n  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_ - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (remaining_bits.test(i)) {\n      position = static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_ - i);\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n  if (position == 0) {\n    position = BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_ + 1;\n  }\n\n  // Update the register with max value (thread-safe)\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  // where alpha = 0.79402 (CONSTANT), m = num_buckets_\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

Parameterized constructor. */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nHyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits)\n    : cardinality_(0), n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {\n  // Handle negative bits - treat as invalid, use 0 buckets\n  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0) {\n    n_leading_bits_ = 0;\n    num_buckets_ = 0;\n  } else {\n    num_buckets_ = static_cast<size_t>(1) << n_leading_bits_;\n  }\n  dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets_, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(0));\n}\n\n/** @brief Element is added for HLL calculation. */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // For Presto HLL, we use the hash directly (64 bits)\n  // Extract bucket index from the leading n_leading_bits_ bits (MSB)\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  if (n_leading_bits_ > 0) {\n    bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits_);\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros in the remaining bits + 1 (position of leftmost 1)\n  // The remaining bits start after the bucket index bits\n  // Create mask to clear the bucket index bits\n  uint64_t remaining_bits = hash;\n  if (n_leading_bits_ > 0 && n_leading_bits_ < 64) {\n    // Clear the top n_leading_bits_ bits\n    remaining_bits = hash << n_leading_bits_;\n  } else if (n_leading_bits_ >= 64) {\n    remaining_bits = 0;\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros and add 1 for the position\n  uint64_t position = 1;\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    // All zeros - maximum position\n    position = 64 - n_leading_bits_ + 1;\n  } else {\n    // Count leading zeros in remaining_bits\n    // __builtin_clzll counts leading zeros for 64-bit\n    int leading_zeros = __builtin_clzll(remaining_bits);\n    position = static_cast<uint64_t>(leading_zeros + 1);\n  }\n\n  // The dense bucket stores lower 4 bits, overflow stores upper 3 bits\n  // Total value is: (overflow << 4) | dense\n  // Max value storable: (7 << 4) | 15 = 127\n\n  // Get current value\n  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();\n  uint64_t current_overflow = 0;\n  if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n    current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)].to_ullong();\n  }\n  uint64_t current_value = (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | current_dense;\n\n  // Only update if new position is greater\n  if (position > current_value) {\n    // Split position into dense (lower 4 bits) and overflow (upper bits)\n    uint64_t new_dense = position & 0xF;                                     // Lower 4 bits\n    uint64_t new_overflow = (position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) & 0x7;           // Next 3 bits\n\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);\n    overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_overflow);\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    // Reconstruct the full value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(i)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(i)].to_ullong();\n    }\n    uint64_t register_val = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      // Position is how many bits from MSB (1-indexed)\n      // bit 63 -> position 1, bit 62 -> position 2, etc.\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - i);\n    }\n  }\n  // If all zeros, return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1 (max position)\n  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the first n_bits_ bits (MSB)\n  // The bucket index is taken from the most significant n_bits_ bits\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  if (n_bits_ > 0) {\n    bucket_idx = hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);\n  }\n\n  // Create remaining bits by shifting out the bucket index bits\n  // The remaining bits are used to count the position of leftmost 1\n  uint64_t remaining_hash = hash;\n  if (n_bits_ > 0 && n_bits_ < BITSET_CAPACITY) {\n    remaining_hash = hash << n_bits_;\n  } else if (n_bits_ >= BITSET_CAPACITY) {\n    remaining_hash = 0;\n  }\n\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining_bits(remaining_hash);\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t position = PositionOfLeftmostOne(remaining_bits);\n\n  // Update the register with max value (thread-safe)\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  // where alpha = 0.79402 (CONSTANT), m = num_buckets_\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  // where alpha = 0.79402 (CONSTANT), m = num_buckets_\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

    "content": "//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n//\n//                         BusTub\n//\n// hyperloglog.cpp\n//\n// Identification: src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp\n//\n// Copyright (c) 2015-2025, Carnegie Mellon University Database Group\n//\n//===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//\n\n#include \"primer/hyperloglog.h\"\n#include <cmath>\n\nnamespace bustub {\n\n/** @brief Parameterized constructor. */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nHyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {\n  // Handle negative bits - treat as invalid, use 0 buckets\n  if (n_bits_ < 0) {\n    n_bits_ = 0;\n    num_buckets_ = 0;\n  } else {\n    num_buckets_ = static_cast<size_t>(1) << n_bits_;\n  }\n  registers_.resize(num_buckets_, 0);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes binary.\n *\n * @param[in] hash\n * @returns binary of a given hash\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {\n  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes leading zeros.\n *\n * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset\n * @returns position of leftmost one bit (1-indexed from MSB)\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 bit (1-indexed from MSB)\n  // Scan from MSB (bit 63) to LSB (bit 0)\n  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      // Position is how many bits from MSB (1-indexed)\n      // bit 63 -> position 1, bit 62 -> position 2, etc.\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - i);\n    }\n  }\n  // If all zeros, return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1 (max position)\n  return BITSET_CAPACITY + 1;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the first n_bits_ bits (MSB)\n  // The bucket index is taken from the most significant n_bits_ bits\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  if (n_bits_ > 0) {\n    bucket_idx = hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);\n  }\n\n  // Create remaining bits by shifting out the bucket index bits\n  // The remaining bits are used to count the position of leftmost 1\n  uint64_t remaining_hash = hash;\n  if (n_bits_ > 0 && n_bits_ < BITSET_CAPACITY) {\n    remaining_hash = hash << n_bits_;\n  } else if (n_bits_ >= BITSET_CAPACITY) {\n    remaining_hash = 0;\n  }\n\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining_bits(remaining_hash);\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t position = PositionOfLeftmostOne(remaining_bits);\n\n  // Update the register with max value (thread-safe)\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[i]));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  // where alpha = 0.79402 (CONSTANT), m = num_buckets_\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

        "   uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;",
        "+  uint64_t remaining_hash = hash;",
        "+",

        "-  if (n_leading_bits_ > 0 && n_leading_bits_ < 64) {",

        "-  }",

HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    // Reconstruct the full value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class the MOST significant n_leading_bits_ bits\n  // - Position is based on leading zeros in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  if (n_leading_bits_ > 0) {\n    bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - bits) and overflow (upper bits)\n    uint64_t new_dense = position & 0xF;                           // Lower 4 bits\n    uint64_t new_overflow = (position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) & 0x7;  // Next 3 bits\n\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);\n    overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_overflow);\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    // Reconstruct the full value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(i)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(i)].to_ullong();\n    }\n    uint64_t register_val = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    // Reconstruct the full value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class negative bits - treat as invalid, use 0 buckets\n  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0) {\n    n_leading_bits_ = 0;\n    num_buckets_ = 0;\n  } else {\n    num_buckets_ = static_cast<size_t>(1) << HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // For Presto HLL:\n  // - Bucket index comes from the MOST significant n_leading_bits_ bits\n  // - Position is calculated from the remaining bits\n  uint64_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  if (n_leading_bits_ > 0) {\n    bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits_);\n  }\n\n  // Shift left to remove bucket bits, then calculate position\n  uint64_t shifted = hash << n_leading_bits_;\n\n  // Calculate position: for non-zero remaining, position = 63 - n_leading_bits - leading_zeros\n  uint64_t position;\n  if (shifted == 0) {\n    // All zeros in remaining - maximum position\n    position = 64 - n_leading_bits_;\n  } else {\n    // Count leading zeros and calculate position\n    int leading_zeros = __builtin_clzll(shifted);\n    position = static_cast<uint64_t>(63 - n_leading_bits_ - leading_zeros);\n  }\n\n  // The dense bucket stores lower 4 bits, overflow stores upper 3 bits\n  // Total value is: (overflow << 4) | dense\n\n  // Get current value\n  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();\n  uint64_t current_overflow = 0;\n  if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n    current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)].to_ullong();\n  }\n  uint64_t current_value = (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | current_dense;\n\n  // Only update if new position is greater\n  if (position > current_value) {\n    // Split position into dense (lower 4 bits) and overflow (upper bits)\n    uint64_t new_dense = position & 0xF;                           // Lower 4 bits\n    uint64_t new_overflow = (position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) & 0x7;  // Next 3 bits\n\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);\n    overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(bucket_idx)] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_overflow);\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (num_buckets_ == 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Calculate harmonic mean of 2^(-register[i])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets_; i++) {\n    // Reconstruct the full value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(i)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(i)].to_ullong();\n    }\n    uint64_t register_val = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  // HyperLogLog formula: E = alpha * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_buckets_);\n  double estimate = CONSTANT * m * m / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

#include "primer/hyperloglog.h"
#include <cmath>

namespace bustub {

/** @brief Parameterized constructor. */
template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // Handle negative or zero bits - treat as invalid, use 0 buckets
  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    n_bits_ = 0;
    num_buckets_ = 0;
  } else {
    num_buckets_ = static_cast<size_t>(1) << n_bits_;
  }
  registers_.resize(num_buckets_, 0);
}

/**
 * @brief Function that computes binary.
 *
 * @param[in] hash
 * @returns binary of a given hash
 */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);
}

/**
 * @brief Function that computes leading zeros.
 *
 * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset
 * @returns leading zeros of given binary set
 */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (counting from LSB starting at 1)
  // We scan from the MSB (position BITSET_CAPACITY-1) down to position 0
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (bset.test(i)) {
      // Position counting from right (LSB=1), so position is i+1
      return static_cast<uint64_t>(i + 1);
    }
  }

 */
template <typename KeyType>

  // Find position of leftmost 1 bit (1-indexed from MSB)
  // Scan from MSB (bit 63) to LSB (bit 0)

    if (bset.test(i)) {
      // Position is how many bits from MSB (1-indexed)
      // bit 63 -> position 1, bit 62 -> position 2, etc.

  if (n_leading_bits_ == 0) {
    remaining = hash;  // All bits are remaining
  } else if (n_leading_bits_ >= 64) {
    remaining = 0;  // No remaining bits
  } else {
    uint64_t mask = (1ULL << (64 - n_leading_bits_)) - 1;
    remaining = hash & mask;
  }

#include <iostream>
#include <cstdint>
#include <bitset>
using namespace std;

using hash_t = size_t;

static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<int8_t>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

template <typename T>
static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));
}

int main() {
    int64_t val = 1;
    hash_t h = Hash(&val);
    cout << "Hash of 1: " << h << endl;
    cout << "Binary: " << bitset<64>(h) << endl;
    
    // Count leading zeros in the hash (from MSB)
    int leading_zeros = 0;
    uint64_t v = h;
    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
        if ((v >> i) & 1) {
            leading_zeros = 63 - i;
            break;
        }
    }
    cout << "Leftmost 1 position from MSB (0-indexed): " << leading_zeros << endl;
    
    // Position from the left = leading_zeros + 1
    cout << "Position of leftmost 1 (1-indexed from MSB): " << (leading_zeros + 1) << endl;
    
    val = -1;
    h = Hash(&val);
    cout << "\nHash of -1: " << h << endl;
    cout << "Binary: " << bitset<64>(h) << endl;
    
    return 0;
}
EOF

#include <iostream>
#include <cstdint>
#include <bitset>
using namespace std;

using hash_t = size_t;

static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<int8_t>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

template <typename T>
static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {
    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));
}

int main() {
    int64_t val = 0;
    hash_t h = Hash(&val);
    cout << "Hash of 0: " << h << endl;
    cout << "Binary: " << bitset<64>(h) << endl;
    
    // n_bits = 3, so 8 buckets
    int n_bits = 3;
    uint64_t bucket_idx = h >> (64 - n_bits);
    cout << "Bucket index (top 3 bits): " << bucket_idx << endl;
    
    uint64_t remaining = h << n_bits;
    cout << "Remaining: " << bitset<64>(remaining) << endl;
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
using namespace std;
typedef size_t hash_t;
int main() {
    int64_t val = -9151314442816847872L;
    hash_t hash = static_cast<hash_t>(val);
    int n_bits = 1;
    
    // Extract from MSB
    uint64_t bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - n_bits);
    cout << "bucket_idx (from MSB): " << bucket_idx << endl;
    
    // Remaining bits (shift left to remove bucket bits, then shift right)
    uint64_t remaining = (hash << n_bits) >> n_bits;  // Clear top bits
    // Or we could shift left then look at leading zeros
    uint64_t shifted = hash << n_bits;
    cout << "shifted: " << bitset<64>(shifted) << endl;
    
    int leading_zeros = __builtin_clzll(shifted);
    cout << "leading zeros in shifted: " << leading_zeros << endl;
    cout << "position (from leading zeros): " << (leading_zeros + 1) << endl;
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
using namespace std;
typedef size_t hash_t;
int main() {
    // Test with 262144
    hash_t hash = 262144;
    int n_bits = 1;
    
    // Extract from MSB
    uint64_t bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - n_bits);
    cout << "hash = " << hash << endl;
    cout << "bucket_idx (from MSB): " << bucket_idx << endl;
    
    // Clear top n_bits and count trailing zeros
    uint64_t mask = (1ULL << (64 - n_bits)) - 1;
    uint64_t remaining = hash & mask;
    cout << "remaining: " << remaining << endl;
    cout << "remaining binary: " << bitset<64>(remaining) << endl;
    int trailing_zeros = __builtin_ctzll(remaining);
    cout << "trailing zeros: " << trailing_zeros << endl;

    bucket_idx = hash >> (64 - n_bits);
    cout << "hash = " << hash << endl;
    cout << "bucket_idx (from MSB): " << bucket_idx << endl;
    
    remaining = hash & mask;

33. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/test9.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
using namespace std;
typedef size_t hash_t;

int getPosition(hash_t hash, int n_bits) {
    if (n_bits == 0) {
        // No bucket bits, use all 64 bits
        if (hash == 0) return 64;
        return __builtin_clzll(hash) + 1;
    }
    
    // Bucket from MSB, remaining shifted left
    uint64_t shifted = hash << n_bits;
    if (shifted == 0) {
        return 64;  // All zeros in remaining
    }
    int leading_zeros = __builtin_clzll(shifted);
    return leading_zeros + 1;
}

int main() {
    // Test 262144 with n_bits=1
    cout << "262144, n_bits=1:" << endl;
    hash_t hash = 262144;
    int n_bits = 1;
    uint64_t bucket = hash >> (64 - n_bits);
    int pos = getPosition(hash, n_bits);
    cout << "bucket: " << bucket << ", position: " << pos << endl;
    cout << "Expected: bucket 0, position 18" << endl;
    
    // Test -9151314442816847872L with n_bits=1
    cout << "\n-9151314442816847872L, n_bits=1:" << endl;
    int64_t val = -9151314442816847872L;
    hash = static_cast<hash_t>(val);
    bucket = hash >> (64 - n_bits);
    pos = getPosition(hash, n_bits);
    cout << "bucket: " << bucket << ", position: " << pos << endl;
    cout << "Expected: bucket 1, position 8" << endl;
    
    return 0;
}
EOF

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
using namespace std;
typedef size_t hash_t;

int main() {
    int64_t val = -1;
    hash_t hash = static_cast<hash_t>(val);
    
    cout << "val: " << val << endl;
    cout << "hash: " << hash << endl;
    cout << "hash binary: " << bitset<64>(hash) << endl;
    
    // bucket from MSB
    uint64_t bucket_idx = hash >> 63;
    cout << "bucket_idx: " << bucket_idx << endl;
    
    // shifted
    uint64_t shifted = hash << 1;
    cout << "shifted: " << bitset<64>(shifted) << endl;

    if (shifted != 0) {
        leading_zeros = __builtin_clzll(shifted);
    }
    cout << "leading_zeros: " << leading_zeros << endl;
    
    // position = 63 - n_bits - leading_zeros = 63 - 1 - 0 = 62
    uint64_t position = 63 - 1 - leading_zeros;
    cout << "position: " << position << endl;
    
    return 0;
}

int main() {

    cout << "n=0, mask: " << mask << endl;
    
    n = 1;

    cout << "n=1, mask: " << mask << endl;

    int trailing_zeros = __builtin_ctzll(remaining);
    cout << "trailing_zeros: " << trailing_zeros << endl;
    
    return 0;
}
